Hlukana Nomzabalazo 

UMbube, Mandlesilo, Mafavuke Mtshali, indodana yomfelokazi uMazwane waseMalukazi, yandwalaza ekilasini. Amehlo kaMbube ayekuNtozonke Nxumalo, kanti ingqondo nemicabango yakhe yayisavakashele uyise emathuneni akwaGijima. Ukuqaqamba kwekhanda kanye noknbaba komlomo yindlala, kwasiilyu ndela isifundo sezenkolo. Imizamo yokuphindela eMbabane noma eHarare yathatha izinyanga ezintathu, oMbube behleli kwaDlamini eKubuta . eSwazini. Babegqigqa begqigqile eposini elalitholakala esitolo, eLudzidzini Mavuso Emporium esasingalena kwentaba iLamgabhi. Ukusuka kwaDlamini kuya esitolo kwakungamakhilomitha acishe abe yishumi nambili uma umuntu ehamba ngezindlela ezinqamulelayo. Noma amahhashi nezimbongolo zazikhona, akekho owayekwazi ukugibela kulezi zinsizwa zamabhasi, zamabhayisikili, zezimoto, zamatekisi kanye nezitimela. Zonke lezi zinto zokuhamba ziyindlala emazweni angaphandle kweNingizimu-Afrika. Imigwaqo nayo ayiminingi. Ngenye inkathi izimoto azihambi ngoba amathayi engekho ezitolo ezidayisa amathayi. Ibanga eliya esitolo lalingabakhathazi oMankanini noQinisela ngoba isizungu sasisho ukuhamba nabo. Babengawatholi amaphepha okufunda, kuthi nalelo elitholakalayo, i-Times of Swaziland, libe nezindaba zaseSwazini, hhayi izindaba abazijahile zaseNingizimu-Afrika. 
    I-Times of Swaziland yayingunyuziphepha ongcono kakhulu kunonyuziphepha baseNingizimu-Afrika ngoba yayivama ukubhala ngezindaba ezakhayo, hhayi ukubhala ngemibolo, udlame nobugebengu njengeningi lamaphepha eseNingizimu-Afrika. Uhambo loMbube besuka eKubuta, eSwazini belibhekise eTanzania Iwazombeleza cishe unyaka. Lwaluhlangabezana nezikhevethe zezimpi, namafindo abavova abashiya bematwayitwayi. Amaphupho okuthi bazongena e-Inhambane baphikelele eSofala, eMarrupa noma eMaedi asala phansi bezithola sebengaphakathi kwezwe elinesibhicongo sempi yombango phakathi kweFrelimo neRenamo eMozambique. Lezi zimpi nezinye ezazibheduke emazweni amaningi ase-Afrika zakuveza ukuthi akukho ukuthula e-Afrika; futhi ayikho nenkululeko emazweni amaningi ase-Afrika. 
   K wembuleka koMbube ukuthi abakhoseli baseNingizimuAfrika babefana nethonsi olwandle lwabakhoseli ababeqile kumamiliyoni amahlanu. Amazwe amaningi ase-Afrika ayekhungathwe yizimpi zemibango ezazidudula izindimbane zamaAfrika ziyowakhoselisa kwamanye amazwe. Ubushokobezi nezimpi zakula mazwe zayinyundela imizamo yemithonselana yabakhoseli baseNingizimu-Afrika. Kwabaningi kwacaca ukuthi kanti imizamo yabo kwezomzabalazo yayingeyona into eqalayo kwezombangazwe, futhi eyabo ingenzima njengezimpi ababehlangana nazo. 
   Yayibambene ngezihluthu e-Angola, eBiafra, eBurundi, eMozambique, eNamibia, eRuwanda naseSomalia. Kwaku-' nezikhukhula zabantu ezazibalekela umbuso' ka-Idi Amin e-Uganda. Yizo lezi zimpi ezazenza ukuba isibalo sabakhoseli senyuke, futhi senze nokuba kudidiyelwe cishe ndawonye

abakhoseli abaphuma ezindaweni ezahlukene. Imizamo yabakhoseli baseNingizimu-Afrika ukuthola usizo kn-United Nations High Commission for Refugees yayingqubuzana nezidingo zala mamiliyoni amahlanu abakhoseli. Abakhoseli baseNingiiimuAfrika ababona izinto kalufifi nakafuphi, abanjengoMankanini, bal?engazicabangi izinkinga zama-Refugee Commissioners, bona befuna ukuba kunakwe bona nje kuphela. K wabaningi base Ningizimu-Afrika kwaphela ukuzikhohlisa nokuzikhukhumeza ngoknthi babeyizi ngqalabutho kwezomzabalazo woknlwela inknluleko. 

   Empeleni kwavela ukuthi abakhoseli baseNingizimu-Afrika babengekho empini, futhi bengayazi ukuthi impi iyini. Izimpi zase-Angola, Biafra, Mozambique, Rhodesia noRuwanda zazihlasimulisa umzimba ngezinkelenkele ezenzeka kula mazwe. Umbango phakathi kwe-MPLA kaMongameli u-Augustino Neto noma uMongameli Joe Eduardo da Santos noJonas Savimbi yabhubhisa yemukisa abantu abeqile ku-800 000. Izimpi ezabaphazamisayo oMbube ohambeni lwabo kwaba yizimpi zaseMozambique. Ukuthola inkululeko kweMozambique aknlethanga uxolo nokuthula, kodwa kwalandelwa yisikhemelele somzila wegazi. 

   Bathi nje sebenezinyanga ezimbili eXai-Xai okuyinhIoko dolobha ye-province yase-Inbambane, eMozambique, kwacaca koMbube ukuthi basengozini enknlu ngenxa yeRenamo. Izakhamuzi zaseMozambique zaziphithizela zibalekela ezinkanjini ziyobhaca. IRenamo yayigasela ngamandla emaphandleni, ngakho-ke izakhamizi zazithuthelana emadolobheni lapho zazithola khona ukubhaca zigadwe ngamasotsha eFrelimo. Ezinye izakhamizi zazibalekela eBotswana, eNingizimu-Afrika, eRhodesia, eSwazini, eTanzania naseZambia. Lokhu kusho uknthi ngenye inkathi babehlangana nemishubo yabakhoseli ilibangise eSwazini noma eNingizimu-Afrika. Okwaknxosha laba bantu eMozambique kwaknyisihlukn seRenamo okwakubikwa uknthi iphoqelela abantu uknba bashiye amakhaya abo, babanqamule izitho zomzimba, futhi babuye bashise imizi yesigodi sonke.

   "Hhawu kahle ukungibangela isieanueanu Qinisela. Ungathini ukuqhathanisa iFrelimo neRenamo?" kubuza yena belu uMankanini. Ungakhohlwa ukuthi uMiguel usevela eNingizimuAfrika lapho ahubula khona imineindo ye-capitalism. Yiyo lena emsanganisayo imhubhuzisa: Mina ngizozinikela kuFrelimo."

Ezomlando ayezifunda azifundisise zazimtshela uMbube ukuthi iMozambique yayingebhekane neNingizimu-Afrika ngezikhali. Futhi-ke uMbube wayekubona ukuthi alikho nelilodwa izwe e-Afrika elalingalwa neNingizimu-Afrika. Ukukhonza kwabo 10 mholi, kwakuletha inkungu eyayikuhwalalisa ukueabanga ngalo mholi nezwe lakhe. Izinkulankula zaseMozambique kwezepolitiki zazilikhalakathisela leli zwe olwembini Iwezingxushungxushu ezidabukisayo. Imizamo kaMbube yokuba baphume eMozambique yayingeke iphumelele uma yayincike ekugudluzeni uMankanini ekukhonzeni uMongameli Samora Maehel. Lokhu kwenza ukuba uMbube afune ezinye izindlela zokubaphephisa ngokuphuma eMozambique. Wayingenisa Ie ndaba ngokuthi, "Bafowethu masingayingeni eyomndeni. Lokho kwakwenza ukuba uMankanini azifunele owakhe uzimele geqe kwanhliziyo ngise. Waqala ukuba angabethembi abaholi bemibutho yangaphandle, futhi angazethembi nezinhlangano ezazizama ukubasiza besemazweni. Ukuba semazweni kwamnika elihle ithuba lokuba aphile impilo ka-angikhathali, anginandaba, 'angincengile ngoba mina ngiyazibusa, futhi angithandi ukuncikiselwa. Noma kunjalo, ukulokozelela, ukufisa nokufuna isigcawu sempi engasitholi kwase kuqala ukumfothoza, ukumchoboza kabuhlungu, kuyicozulula inkani, intshisakalo nokwethemba. Yizikhathi zokuthula nokucabanga ezinjengaleso ezazimthunuka uMankanini azizwe ephelelwa ngamandla okushofuza, ukucula nokugiya. Noma kunjalo, izicathami zaseNingizimu-Afrika zazisabazingela abakhoseli abaqhamuka eNingizimu-Afrika. Amahemuhemu ayethi kwase kunabantu ababezama ukuhogela umkhondo wabo. K wezwakala futhi nokuthi kwakunabeLungu ababeloku. bethatha oMbube izithombe ebholeni. Abakhoselisi balezi zinsizwa bazidonsa ngendlebe bazeluleka ukuba ziphume ziphele eShamva, futhi zilifulathele elaseZimbabwe ziyobhaca emajukujukwini ezinkangala zasemaphandleni. K wabanzima ukuba babaleke oMbube ngoba basebazi ukuthi kuza uBob Marley ukuzocula ngo-Aprili. Phela iRhodesia yayizophela ngo-Aprili bese kuqala iZimbabwe, izwe elisha. K wezwakala ukuthi njengoba uBob Marley wayezocula emkhosini wenkululeko yaseZimbabwe, wayezomema izindimbane zabantu eziqhamuka eNingizimuAfrika. Namaphoyisa aseNingizimu-Afrika ayezothatha lelo thuba ukuthola abakhoseli ayekade ebafuna. 

   Isimo sashuba kwabonakala ukuthi uma bengabaleki bayobhaca oMbube, balinde amathonsi abanzi. Omunye umdlali webhola uKarikoga Zvinavashe wabakhipha ngesikabhadakazi enkomponi. Bahamba ngezamahubo bathubeleza ubusuku bonke

Kwathi kusa, basebehambile impela. K wadingeka kuba balale ekuseni, babuye baqhubeke emini sebezothola izimoto, ikakhulu amathilakhi asebenzisa umgwaqo obheke eNyakatho yaseMozambique. ngesikhathi abomDabu baseRhodesia belwa nombuso kaSmith. Wayezimisele ukuwelela eTanzania uGamucharai ngoba ethi kobalukhuni ukuba oMankanini bathole impatho engcono bengazazi izilimi zaseTanzania. Baphumake ngolwesiBili belibhekise emingceleni yaseMozambique bethemba ukuthi kothi kuphela isonto bayobe bengena eNyamafanda besebedlulela eMozambique ngelilandelayo isonto. Esikhundleni salezi zinjwayezi, kwase kwande izinkonono nokutetema kuMankanini, ebalisa ngemvula ena njalo, ilanga lonke, ebalisa ngokushisa, abuye abalise nangesivivi somoya owomisa arnakhala. Wayekhala ekhononda ngempukuvane (tsetse fly). Ukhevethe lwempi lwalungarnesabisi uMankanini kodwa ukungethembi lesi simo sezulu kwasekumthuthumelisa. 

   Wayesedaxazela nje uMankanini ezihudula ngosizi olugodle ukwesaba okunarnandla nokukhathazeka nendumalo eyayimgwaza ezibilini. Wazarna ukukuphebeza lobu buthakathaka uGamucharai ngokumgxobela ijalaphi (moon creepers) kanye nehlozi elimhlophe (mikania capenses). Larna khathakhatha enqaba ukumelapha uMankanini. Nezijabane zikaGarnucharai kazibanga namandla, ngenxa yoharnbo nokulala emahlathini kwabakhoseli. Khona babeke banetha izinsuku, kodwa bengakushayi mkhuba lokho ngoba kwakujwayelekile. Impilo ebuthaka yabaphoqelela ukuba bangenise emzini othile. Bemukelwe kahle kulo muzi noma nawo wawungenabo abantu besilisa beloku besemahlathini. Lazulazula ibhanoyi phezulu emoyeni lilindele ukungena e-J F Kennedy Airport, eNew York. Amaphaphu kaMbube ayephezulu engakholwa kahle ukuthi ngempela usephumile e-Afrika wafika ezweni lenkululeko, lobungane nengcebo ayehlala eyibukela kude. Ukulunguza ngaphansi kwamkhombisa lesi sithabathaba sedolobhakazi elaliqabulana ne-Atlantic Ocean, futhi linamachibi neziqhingi eziningi. Esesemkhathini wakwelamela ukuthi iziqhingi eziningi zazihlanganiswa ngamabhuloho amade ayenemishubo yezimoto okungathi zihamba ngazine, noma nganhlanu ngokulinganisana. Noma wayeke wafunda ngo-Oval Island, Long Island no-St John Island yayingekho indlela yokwazi ukuthi zazikuphi lezi ziqhingi, ngisho nokwazi ukuthi iNew York iqalaphi igcinaphi. Kuye emoyeni, leli dolobhakazi lalifana nje nolwandle olungenamkhawulo. Ingqikithi yemicabango yakhe yayijikeleza emazwini athi, "Free at last!" 

   Ngempela wayezizwa esekhululekile esefike eMelika, kuhulumeni omkhulu owayengeke ayidedele iNingizimu-Afrika ukuba igcogcome ezweni lakhe izingela abakhoseli baseNingizimu-Afrika. Kulelo gagasi lentokozo nenkululeko, uMbube wafikelwa ukukhumbula uNtozonke. Wayaluzisa amehlo efuna ukubona isithombe sentokazi yenkululeko (liberty tower) kodwa wehluleka. Wakhuluma yedwa wathi, "Akunani ntokazi, ngozifikela kuwe ngelinye ilanga sengihamba noNtozonlee. Ngenye imini songena eNew York noNtozonlee ngaleli bhanoyi eliphuma e-Afrika. Ungilinde Ntozonke. Ngobuya ngikulande ngane yabantu."

Waphuma emhhumeni waselinda abakhoseli ababili baseNingizimu-Afrika nabo ababezokhosela eMelika. Laba bakhoseli kwakungumnumzane uPhilani Njokwe nowakwakhe uMaMpofu. UMaMpofu wayezithwele, futhi engaphilile kahle. K wadingeka ukuba bamtholele isitulo esinamasondo (wheel chair) ephuma ebhanoyini.     Baphindela kuJeffersen Road benyuka naye aze aqala ukuphela ama-apartments. Ngokuphela kwama-apartments yaqala futhi leya mizi ecinene yezitini ababeyibone bengena eChicago. Wakhumbuia izingane zasekhaya eNingizimuAfrika zidlala ibhola nomagalopha ezikhaleni nasemigwaqeni. 

    Bathi bangeqa u-91 st A venue base beyimisa imoto bapaka phambi kwendlu eyayingu nombolo-3436. Kwakungathi uyaphupha uMbube efikela ekhaya labantu basekhaya eNingizimu-Afrika. Njengokujwayelekile, ubaba wekhaya wazihlabisa isivakashi eziqhamuka eNingizimu-Afrika. Imizi yaseMelika iba namakamela angaphansi komhlaba abizwa ngokuthi ngama-basements: La makamelo asetshenziswa kakhulu uma kunesiphepho esimukisa imizi. Imbuzi eyayizohlatshwa yayibekwe khona e-basement. UMondise wangenisa uMbube ngokuthi, "Nanti izinyane esikwamukela ngalo Hlabangane, Magalela gase onjengengonyama. Kwaphela amasonto amabili uMbube eseYunivesithi yaseMichigan ejwayeziswa izindawo nendlela okusetshenzwa ngayo kule yunivesithi. Ukujwayeziswa (orientation) kwakuhlelwe ngale ndlela yokuba abafundi .abasha bahlanganiswe bese bejwayeziswa bengamaqembu abafundi abayishuminanhlanu. Lilinye iqembu laliba n<imholi ongumfundi omdala wale yunivesithi. Eqenjini likaMbube kwakunamaShayina amathathu, amaJaphani amabili, abaseKhoriya abathathu, owase-Indonesia oyedwa, kanye namaMelikana amhlophe. KwakunguMbube yedwa omnyama, futhi wase-Afrika kuleli qembu lokujwayeziswa uMbube. 
   Wayethi uma ekhuluma umholi wabo okunye kubalahlekele abafundi abaphuma ngaphandle kwaseMelika, noma abafundi bezizwe ngezizwe, njengoba babebizwa kanjalo kule yunivesithi. Babebona nje ngamaMelikana esehleka ukuthi lokho okukhulunywayo yihlaya. UMbube wayesazi isiNgisi, engafani nakancane nabafundi base-Asia. Yindlela nje eyekhuluma tigayo amaMelikana eyayisamdida. Wakuphawula ukuthi amaMelikana akhulumela phansi, azigwinye futhi ezinye izinhlamvu zamagama. Wazimisela ukuba naye azame ukucosha masinyane ngoba wayengekwamukele neze ukuba alahlekelwe yimfundo yakhe. ngenxa nje yokuthi kezwa kahle ukuthi kuthiwani. Kwamduduza uMbube ukubona ukuthi abase-Asia babengasazi isiNgisi, befunda nendlela yokubhala ehlukile kweyakubo, kodwa bengazibekile phansi. Ngenxa yokuthi uMbube namaShayina babeyimiphuma, bajwayelana nebhungu lomShayina, uLee Chen. Lobu bungane bakhe noLee babakhana ngoba uLee wayefuna ukufunda isiNgisi

   Kwathi kuphela amasonto amabili okuj~ayezisa abafundi, uMbube wabe eseyibona imfihlo yempumelelo yasemayunivesithi aseMelika. Lapha izinto zazenziwa ngenye indlela, kungashaphuluzwa nje. Imfundo noma ezemidlalo zazihlablelwa kable umfundi azame ukuzilolonga kabanzi ngolwazi oluthile angav~ vanyiswa ashaphuluziswe yonke indawo. K wamkhanyela uMbube ukuthi imfundo yaseNingizimu-Afrika kwakungumashwaphuluza kokunyantalaza nje, umfundi evavanya lOnke izinto kanyekanye esikhundleni sokuba agogode emakbonweni athile, awasebenzise lawo makbono njengezitini lOkwakbela phezu kwazo. Wakubona ukuthi okuningi ayethi uyakwazi, kwakulOdingeka ukuba akuqale phansi, akuhlablele kable, besefuna izindlela lOkuqoqoda isitho nesitho ngasinye. Wayengasafuni nokuthi uyalazi ibhola lezinyawo ngoba kwamkhanyela ukuthi wayengalifundanga kahle. Wayebhamuza njengeningi labadlali ekbaya uNingizimu-Afrika. 
    Phakathi kwezifundo zakbe ezaziyimpoqo kwaba yikilasi lokubhala (writing skills). Bengakaqali la makilasi wayengazi nje ukuthi yini eyezoyifunda ngoba yena wayethi useyakwazi' ukubhala. Leli kilasi lamfundisa ukuthi ukubhala kuza ngezigamu eziyisithupha: okungukukbetha isihloko, ukuqoqa iminingwane ozobhala ngayo, ukuhlela, ukubhala kokuqala (prewriting), ukubukeza, ukulolonga osekubhaliwe, bese kukbane kuba ngukubhala kwangempela. Le nto yakbe neningi labafundi baseNingizimu-Afrika yokuba bavele bagxambukele nje ekuklwiklwizeni kwernibhalo besebehambisa kothisha ngoba bethi baqedile kodwa bengakaqali, wayiyeka uMbube. Wasekwazi manje ukukbetha isihloko, azi ukuthi leso sihloko sirnnandi sivumelana nesikbathi anaso, ulwazi analo kanye nezirihlos~ zakbe. Bathi bephakathi naleli kilasi wabona uMbube ukuthi ezikoleni zaseNingizimu-Afrika bona babegcina ku (prewriting) bese besa into eluhlaza kothisha. Wawungabukezwa, ungalolongwa, futhi ungabhalwa okokugcina umsebenzi njengoba kusho izincwadi lOkubhala. Wazinikeza isikbathi eside sokubukeza uMbube, awulolonge futhi awubhale kabusha okokugcina njalo umsebenzi wakbe. 
94 
   Leli kilasi lokubhala laba ngumgogodla wemfundo yakbe, lakucacisa ukuthi iningi labafundi baseNingizimu-Afrika babemfundomfushane ngenxa yobudedengu obusekufundisem ukubhala. Eyunivesithi ayekuyo kwakubasiza abafundi. ukuba kbona kwabeluleki ababehlalele nje ukusiza abafundi ngamakbono okubhala. Umfundi wayeshaya ucingo enze uhlelo lokubonana nensizakubhala. Lezi nsizakubhala zazihlala nalowo mfundi bese zikufunda okubhaliwe, zimluleke umfundi ngendlela yakbe yokubhala. Babemkbombisa lokbo akwenza kable, bese bemtshengisa nezibhobo ezidinga ukwelashwa ukuze ukubhala kwakbe kusumame. UMbube wayekbombisa ukuba namaxhwala amaningi ekubhaleni kwakhe esaqala ukuthola usizo ezinsizenikubhala. K wathi sekuyophela izinyanga ezintathu wayesengcono kakbulu, futhi naye esezizwa elaphekile. 
   Ngokufunda noLee kanye namanye amaShayina, uMbube katholanga bunzima ezifundweni zakbe zesayensi. Kwamkhuthaza kakbulu ukuthi koPhysics neMathemalics wayeseqophelweni eliphezulu ngoba iGPA (grade average point) yakbe yayingu-3.87. Okwenza lokho kwaba yiyo indlela yokwenza konke ngenkumbula yamagalelo aphuma eukumbuleni yezincwadi. Wayeyeneka igcwale itafula irniqingo yamabhuku ukuze ezwe ukuthi izifundiswa ezahlukene ziyibeka kanjani leyo nto ayifundayo. Wayeziqhathanisa lezi zifundiswa azidedele ukuba zikbulurnisane noma ziphikisane. Wayenganeliswa ukuthi into useyayazi uma efunde izincwadi ezimbili noma ezintathu ngento eyodwa. Ngenxa yolimi, uLee yena wayengasheshi uma efunda, ngakbo ezifundela izincwadi ezimbalwa besekuthola kuMbube okuningi abakufundayo.

   Ukujwayela eMelika kwanika uMbube ithuba lokuba aqale ukusebenza andise kule mali. engu-$7oo ngenyanga ayeyithola kumfundaze wakhe. Umsebenzi wakhe wokuqala kwakungukugeza izitsha ehhotela laseyunivesithi. Wayesebenza amahora angu-20 ngeviki, ehola $6 ngehora. Kwaya wabuye wacosha namanye amahora angu-20 ngokuba yinsiza kaphulofesa eyunivesithi, umsebenzi owawukhokha $1,200-00 ngenyanga. Kwakwenzeka ngolwesiNe ngo-l kwesikabhadakazi ukuba bethule izimpahla eziza esitolo ababefundela kuso. Wawukhokha $10 ngehora 10 mseberizi kanti babesebenza amahora amane. Le misebenzi yamvumela ukuba athenge eyakhe imoto uMbube ukuze akwazi ukuya emsebenzini kalula. Phela uLee waye ngasebenzi ngoba wayephuma ekhaya elidla kusale. UMbube wawuyeka umsebenzi wokwethula izimpalda ngeukathi esethola umsebenzi okhokha kangcono futhi olula e-GM (General Motors). 

   Kwathi kuphela unyaka wasine uMbube wayesiyiukakha, eseyazi youke iriqubo yaseMelika, futhi negazi lakhe selizithambela iziukambiso zaleli zwe kanye nendlela elaliphatha ngayo aboMdabu base-Afrika. Wayeyazi indawo yaboMdabu baseAfrika ukuthi babedelelekile, bebandlululwa, futhi bekhonjiswa ngezindlela eziningi ukuthi baqhamuka ezweni elibukelwa phansi, izwe lezilwane, lendlala, nezimpi. AboMdabu base-Afrika babengathandeki ngisho nakwabamnyama baseMelika, bona ababeqhakambisa ukuthi aboMdabu base-Afrika bakhuluma nge-accent. Emsebenzini kwa-GM lapho kwenziwa khona izimoto wayekuphawula uMbube ukuthi ungowezizwe, ngakho. impatho yakhe kwakungefanele abantu bokufika. Impatho yayiyimbi ngempela naseyunivesithi ngoba aboMdabu base-Afrika babenqwabelana kule misebenzi eyayingathandwa ngabaseMelika, imisebenzi engakhokhi kalde, enukayo, eshisayo, engcolile kanye neyisicefe. 

   Yikho lokhu okwakwenza ukuba ama-Afrika anqwabelane ekugezeni izitsha, ekukhilineni izindlu zangasese kanye neminye imisebenzi yokufukuza. Othisha, nophulofesa basemayunivesithi ase-Afrika babengabhekelwa imisebenzi ethile uma befika emayunivesithi aseMelika. Babedidiyelwa ndawonye nabanye abafukuzi abasebancane ngeminyaka nangensebenzo.

   Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi uMbube wazithola sebehamba noTiffany njalo uma beya eFlint bayohlela imininingwane yocwaningo Iwezifo zenhliziyo. Futhi babehamba ngemoto kaTiffany ngoba uTiffany wayethi uMbube ushayela kungathi ushayela inqola. Wacimeza uMandla okumuntu ogaselwa iminjunju ezibilini. Wabhavumulisa okwebhobhodlelana elingenwa yidlozi noma okwensizwa ehlaselwa yiphupho elibi. Walizwa elamajikanezwe kuleli culo lamcasula. Wafikelwa ukuthi laba bafundeli babengayazi into ababecula ngayo njengeningi labantu ongalizwa likhuluma lize likhihlize amathe kodwa libe lingayazi into elikhuluma ngayo. Yena njengejikanezwe langempela, akayishayanga mkhuba Ie .ngoma ngoba ubuyena basebuyintandela kuNtozonke. Wayefuna ukuzizwela kahle ngomlomo kaNtozonke lokhu ayehlangabezene nakho. Wasondela kancane kuNtozonke wabuye wambuza futhi wathi, "Uthini Ntozonke? Uthi uyashada? Kodwa ungayenza kanjani into enjengaleyo? Uthi ngingadabula amazwe ngibuyela wena kanti usungibekele induku emqubeni? Cha ngeke neze . ukwenze kimi lokho Ntozonke." 
    K wabanokuthula isikhashana ngemuva kwalokho. Nonyezi waphuma kwangathi nawo uzozibonela Ie nsambatheka. Nokube wayethanda, efuna efisa ukuchaza uNtozonke, ingqondo nemizwa yakhe yayiphithene kangokuba wayengekho esimweni sokuba abumbe into ezwakalayo masishane. Inkukhu yamane yanqunywa umlomo nje. Wazibamba izinyembezi ezaziphokophelele. ukuqubuka zinqande usizi olwaseluthanda ukuphenduka intukuthelo nolaka. engangabazi ukuthi ingaphakathi lakhe lonke lalisamthanda, kwamvadlaza kwaphela nasozwaneni. Izandla zikaNtozonke zazijuluka futhi zivevezela kanti nesifuba sasibhakuzela. Ngemuva kweminyaka eyishumi nanye bahlukana oMandla Mtshali noNtozonke Nxumalo, uMandla wambona uNtozonke esengelihle ipatshaza lentokazi eyayisifuba sigcwele. Izindebe zakhe zazishiya umfanekiso owawuba nevuso lenkumbulo. Wayezisebenzisa lezi zindebe, enganqeni uma ekhuluma, ikakhnlu lapho ebiza izinhlamvu ezingo "sh". Wafa uMankanini eTanzania, wabuyela emuva eNingizimu-Afrika uQinisela kodwa mina ngenqaba ukufa ngakwenqaba nokubuyela ekhaya' ngingakazilungiseleli wena Ntozonke.    Ukufika kukaMandla nazo zonke lezi ndaba ezazilakanyiswa phezu kwakhe kwakumqeda amandla uMaZwane. Wakwazi nokho ukulandela uMandla eya emotweni.    Njengoba wayeseya esitolo, uMandla wacela ukwazi izimpahla ezidliwayo unina eyengase azidinge. Waqala-ke ukwenza uhla lwezinto ayezoya kozithenga ngalesosikhathi ekuseni laphaya ezitolo zaseMlazi noma zaseSiphingo. Noma wayengavumi kahle uMaZwane, bayenza ilisti yezinto lezo.

ukuba ihambise incwadi iyise kwaNxumalo, iyinike usisi wakhona uNtozonke, kodwa abanlu abadala bangayiboni Ie ncwadi. Yahamba-ke Ie ngane ilokhu ibuka udoli wayo. Kayibanga nabunzima ekutholeni uNtozonke ngoba izincwadi zazifika; abantu bethumela amakhadi omshado ubuthaphuthaphu. Kwamshayisa uvalo uNtozonke ukuhluka kwale ncwadi kwezinye izincwadi. Ntambama ngehora lesithupha uMandla nomngane wakhe uRamothibi babenendumezulu yedili elalenzelwe uRamothibi eHoliday Inn Garden Court. Kwamthokozisa uMandla ukubona abomDabu beyiphethe ngobunono yonke imisebenzi yaleli hhotela. K wathi lapho eliqhathanisa leli hhotela nezindawo ayezijwayele eMelika, walifumanisa nalo lisezingeni eliphezulu. Abantu babenyathelana, ikakhulukazi abantu ababenobungane obuxhumene khona ngale kwezilwandle. Babebodwa ababegcinane koSoviet, abanye bagcinane koNew York noma koTanzania. K wamthokozisa uMandla ukubona abazali bomfowabo nabo abamemukela okwendodana yabo. Kulokhu kujabula, abantu abadala babonga abantababo ngokuba babuye bazohlwaya omakoti ngasekhaya. Unina kaRamothibi walibeka ngesihloko elokuthi, "Thina bantabethu sithanda omakoti abazosibheka nathi njengoba siphelelwa ngamandla. Izingane zasemazweni ziyezikhohlwe yithina, kube sengath! nina naqhamuka ezihlahleni. Idili laphela sekusa ngehora lesibili. Lokhu kwenza ukuba oMandla baphuze ukulala. URamothibi warnxoxela uMandla ukuthi bonke abangani bakhe nezintombi ayezazi zasezagana, kanti ezinye zase nje ziphuphile. Wakusho nokuthi iningi lontanga yakhe babengakunakekeli ukwenza ukuba imizimba yabo ingawavumeli amafutha. lningi labo lalibikizela ngukukhuluphala. K wakuzomthalha isikhathi impela ukuthola umuntu ayengathi uyamenelisa. UMandla wamtshela ngolangaliphuma wakwaXaba eBB eMlazi. UMandla waqinisa kumngane wakhe ngokuthi izintombi zikhona eThekwini. Zinde zilapha, zinswazi ezesulekile okungathi zikhafulwa lulwandle.

Wakuphawula nokho ukuthi kwakunezimpawu eziyindida kulolu daba. Intokozo kaMandla yayingaphelele njengoba yayiye igewale uma ekhuluma ngoNtozonke. Yamxaka uRamothibi Ie nto yokuba uMandla aphuthume masisha kangaka umshado, kanti babezohlala inyanga eNingizimu-Afrika. Wayethi uma embuza ukuthi utheni uNtozonke ngezindadatho abamthengela zona eCalifornia, uMandla athi ubengakamtshengisi. Akamgubhanga nokho uRamothibi ngoba wayazi ukuthi umngane wakhe wayenezinWelo eziqondile okothi lomkhonto. 
   Lathi lishaya ihora lesibili ekuseni ngoMgqibelo yaphuma imoto kaRamothibi eGoli isilibangise eMdubane. K wathi kusa yayiphuma eMgungundlovu imoto ibheke koCamperdown. Ngehora lesishiyagalombili oMandla noRamothibi babeqeda ukudla eMaharani. Bagqoka baeonsa baqonda emotweni yabo. Le mota kaRamothibi yayingeono kakhulu kuneCadillae kaMandla. Ubuhle beCeliea babungamemezi kanti obe Cadillae babumemeza buWuthula izintamo zabantu baphenduke nayo bezama ukuthola ukuthi motoni lena. Njengoba iCadillae yayisele egaraji ngenkathi uMandla ebamba indiza eya eGoli, kwadingeka ukuba baqale ngakhona egaraji ukuze bakwazi ukushiya iCeliea bathathe iCadillae. 
   Ilanga lalinsasa libakhumbuza laba bafo koMiami. Baluvula ukhakhayi IweCadillae, basebeehoma ifulege laseMelika ekhaleni layo imoto. Yasuka kaneane isibheke esikhumulweni sezindiza eThekwini. Babengathanda ukuthi lithi liflka ibhanoyi elivela eMauritius besebekhona belilindile. Ngeshwa elijwayelekile, laphuza ukuflka leli bhanoyi kwaze kwacishe kwashaya ihora leshumi. Kwehla izindimbane zabantu kuleli bhanoyi, oMandla noRamothibi abatshenangwa muntu ukuthi nangu uBangenzile. Wayegqamile uBangenzile, kuligeokama lembulunga; eehitha

   "Ukhona 10 mfana karnzala uJele. Uma 10 mfundisi eqinisa ikhanda, sizornxosha aphume lapha esontweni, besekuthi 10 mfana karnzawethu abeseqhuba 10 meimbi. Ake ngikhulume naye nami. Mfundisi kade sipheka silungiselela 10 mshado. Kunezihlobo eziphuma eMaIawi, eGoli, eZambia nakoLiverpool phesheya. Uma uthi 10 mshado uyahlehla uqonde ukuthi laba bantu mabaphindele emuva? Uzozikhokha yini izindleko zabo beza lapha?" 

   Akuqondakali ukuthi ugogo ongumisi Mthethwa wafika kanjani phezulu esiteji. Njengomuntu owayethintene kakhulu nabakwaNxumalo naye wayesebeka umbono ethi, "Kahleni bazali ukujaha nonise uNtozonke. Masilinde uMadoda uzophuma ejele beseqhubeka nomsha .... " 

   "Kable ukusibhedele weMaMthethwa!" kumemeza omunye wonina abaneane bakaNtozonke. "Ubani nje othe Ie ndaba sekungeyesikole manje. Yehlika usuka uphele lapha." Wahudula isishwapha uMiss Mthethwa esehla esiteji. 

   Umfundisi yena waehaya izandla wakuphebeza ukukhokha ngokuthi, "Anginakuzikhokha, zokhokhwa ngabakwaNdimande abephule usuku 10 mshado," kusho yena b

pressure, waqweba umfundisi wasethi Kubheka, nanti nelanga liyashona."
